In particular firefox.exe always opens updater.exe on updates, and then inside updater.cpp we determine if the service should be used. firefox.exe will pick if it wants to use the service by writing pending-service in the update.status fi
  1193. # [16:53] <bbondy> le. And then in updater.cpp we do several checks to see if it should be used, or silently fallback to updating with uac.
